${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k}{-{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}}{-{{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}}}$

${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$ ; ${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _j} _l}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} = {{{{ \gamma} _i} _j}{-{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}}$;${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}} + {{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ d} _k} _j} _l}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}}$
symmetrizing indexes
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{-1}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{-1}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,r}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ d} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{-1}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}$

Riemann curvature
${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

Ricci curvature

using ${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

using Ricci definition

d\hat{d}_{xyz}_dz + -2. * \gamma^{xz} * \gamma^{yz} * d\hat{d}_{yxz}_dz + -2. * \gamma^{yy} * \gamma^{zz} * d\hat{d}_{yzz}_dy + 2. * \gamma^{yy} * \gamma^{zz} * d\hat{d}_{zyz}_dy + 2. * \gamma^{yy} * d\hat{d}_{zxy}_dz)) / 2.;
deriv->Z_x = Z_x * {b^x}_x + Z_y * {b^y}_x + Z_z * {b^z}_x + -K^{xx} * \alpha * d_{xxx} + -K^{yy} * \alpha * d_{xyy} + -K^{zz} * \alpha * d_{xzz} + K_{xx} * \alpha * a^x + K_{xy} * \alpha * a^y + K_{xz} * \alpha * a^z + -\Theta * \alpha * a_x + -\alpha * a_x * {K_x}^x + -\alpha * a_y * {K_x}^y + -\alpha * a_z * {K_x}^z + \alpha * d_x * {K_x}^x + \alpha * d_y * {K_x}^y + \alpha * d_z * {K_x}^z + -2. * K^{xy} * \alpha * d_{xxy} + -2. * K^{xz} * \alpha * d_{xxz} + -2. * K^{yz} * \alpha * d_{xyz} + -2. * K_{xx} * \alpha * e^x + 2. * K_{xx} * \alpha * {d_x}^{xx} + -2. * K_{xy} * \alpha * e^y + -2. * K_{xz} * \alpha * e^z + 2. * K_{yy} * \alpha * {d_x}^{yy} + 2. * K_{zz} * \alpha * {d_x}^{zz} + -2. * Z_x * \alpha * {K_x}^x + -2. * Z_y * \alpha * {K_x}^y + -2. * Z_z * \alpha * {K_x}^z + 4. * K_{xy} * \alpha * {d_x}^{xy} + 4. * K_{xz} * \alpha * {d_x}^{xz} + 4. * K_{yz} * \alpha * {d_x}^{yz} + -8. * S_x * \alpha * M_PI;
deriv->Z_y = Z_x * {b^x}_y + Z_y * {b^y}_y + Z_z * {b^z}_y + -K^{xx} * \alpha * d_{yxx} + -K^{yy} * \alpha * d_{yyy} + -K^{zz} * \alpha * d_{yzz} + K_{xy} * \alpha * a^x + K_{yy} * \alpha * a^y + K_{yz} * \alpha * a^z + -\Theta * \alpha * a_y + -\alpha * a_x * {K_x}^y + -\alpha * a_y * {K_y}^y + -\alpha * a_z * {K_y}^z + \alpha * d_x * {K_x}^y + \alpha * d_y * {K_y}^y + \alpha * d_z * {K_y}^z + -2. * K^{xy} * \alpha * d_{yxy} + -2. * K^{xz} * \alpha * d_{yxz} + -2. * K^{yz} * \alpha * d_{yyz} + 2. * K_{xx} * \alpha * {d_y}^{xx} + -2. * K_{xy} * \alpha * e^x + -2. * K_{yy} * \alpha * e^y + 2. * K_{yy} * \alpha * {d_y}^{yy} + -2. * K_{yz} * \alpha * e^z + 2. * K_{zz} * \alpha * {d_y}^{zz} + -2. * Z_x * \alpha * {K_x}^y + -2. * Z_y * \alpha * {K_y}^y + -2. * Z_z * \alpha * {K_y}^z + 4. * K_{xy} * \alpha * {d_y}^{xy} + 4. * K_{xz} * \alpha * {d_y}^{xz} + 4. * K_{yz} * \alpha * {d_y}^{yz} + -8. * S_y * \alpha * M_PI;
deriv->Z_z = Z_x * {b^x}_z + Z_y * {b^y}_z + Z_z * {b^z}_z + -K^{xx} * \alpha * d_{zxx} + -K^{yy} * \alpha * d_{zyy} + -K^{zz} * \alpha * d_{zzz} + K_{xz} * \alpha * a^x + K_{yz} * \alpha * a^y + K_{zz} * \alpha * a^z + -\Theta * \alpha * a_z + -\alpha * a_x * {K_x}^z + -\alpha * a_y * {K_y}^z + -\alpha * a_z * {K_z}^z + \alpha * d_x * {K_x}^z + \alpha * d_y * {K_y}^z + \alpha * d_z * {K_z}^z + -2. * K^{xy} * \alpha * d_{zxy} + -2. * K^{xz} * \alpha * d_{zxz} + -2. * K^{yz} * \alpha * d_{zyz} + 2. * K_{xx} * \alpha * {d_z}^{xx} + -2. * K_{xz} * \alpha * e^x + 2. * K_{yy} * \alpha * {d_z}^{yy} + -2. * K_{yz} * \alpha * e^y + -2. * K_{zz} * \alpha * e^z + 2. * K_{zz} * \alpha * {d_z}^{zz} + -2. * Z_x * \alpha * {K_x}^z + -2. * Z_y * \alpha * {K_y}^z + -2. * Z_z * \alpha * {K_z}^z + 4. * K_{xy} * \alpha * {d_z}^{xy} + 4. * K_{xz} * \alpha * {d_z}^{xz} + 4. * K_{yz} * \alpha * {d_z}^{yz} + -8. * S_z * \alpha * M_PI;
